              <span id="reviewTextContainer214357621" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7372852193227973524">The thrust of Professor Finkelstein's book is that powerful interests (Israel and Jewish organizations in America) have hijacked what has become known as the holocaust. And while Israel has exploited the holocaust as a weapon to deflect criticism, regardless how justified, American Jewish organizations have used the plight of supposedly needy survivors to extort staggering sums of money from the rest of the world. This was done not for the benefit of survivors, but for the financial advantage of</span>
  <span id="freeText7372852193227973524" style="display:none">The thrust of Professor Finkelstein's book is that powerful interests (Israel and Jewish organizations in America) have hijacked what has become known as the holocaust. And while Israel has exploited the holocaust as a weapon to deflect criticism, regardless how justified, American Jewish organizations have used the plight of supposedly needy survivors to extort staggering sums of money from the rest of the world. This was done not for the benefit of survivors, but for the financial advantage of these organizations.<br />There are no conclusions reached in Professor Finkelstein's book that a careful reader of daily newspapers could not have reached, assuming the reader could read between the lines and base his judgment on evidence and common sense rather than the politically correct slant of the media reporting.<br /><br />Finkelstein has infuriated his critics not by ranting or raving or misrepresenting the evidence, as they have accused him, but by painstakingly supporting his arguments with irrefutable documentation. The first line of defense of the mass media in America, one of the holocaust industry's most effective and compliant tools (second only to the Clinton administration), was to pretend Finkelstein's book did not exist. Once this tactic became ineffective due to an outpouring of Internet exposure, the mass media launched scathing attacks on the author and his book. Read the New York Times book review for one such "hit piece" and compare that review with your own reading of the book. Naturally, reading the book is something the review is designed to discourage.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7372852193227973524" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_3046865514" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3046865514" />
    <a title="☺" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/46840194"><img alt="☺" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1441887162p2/46840194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3046865514?book_show_action=true">Nov 16, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☺" class="user" itemprop="url" name="☺" href="/user/show/46840194">☺</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3046865514" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer14436579120421486295">Concise, highly readable, a 200-note bibliography: <i>The Holocaust Industry</i> is all a scientific-ideological weapon needs to be. I was unaware how recent and artificial the hegemonic Holocaust narrative is, nor how vast the amounts of money (tens of billions of dollars) funnelled into Israel and hazbara, under the aegis of the US. It made me reconsider the political reaction to Jan T Gross' work on Polish complicity in the holocaust, as well as other similar cases.<br/><br/>Finkelstein only really falls flat</span>
  <span id="freeText14436579120421486295" style="display:none">Concise, highly readable, a 200-note bibliography: <i>The Holocaust Industry</i> is all a scientific-ideological weapon needs to be. I was unaware how recent and artificial the hegemonic Holocaust narrative is, nor how vast the amounts of money (tens of billions of dollars) funnelled into Israel and hazbara, under the aegis of the US. It made me reconsider the political reaction to Jan T Gross' work on Polish complicity in the holocaust, as well as other similar cases.<br /><br />Finkelstein only really falls flat in two respects: the agency of western finance and the culprits in the Holocaust Industry. To Finkelstein, all money extorted from Swiss banks and German industry was claimed against their will, only under the pressure of the US. Be that as it may, Western finance is itself very heavily implicated in the propping up of Israel - the narrative of a greedy zionist lobby versus a pragmatic banking sector falls flat. In one case, he appears to be defending Bayer against the accusation that the company directly instigated Mengele's experiments. However, Bayer's backers were 100% instrumental in the rise of the NSDAP and the fascist war machine; their money should not go to Israel, but they are not 'victims' in the story. Secondly, the Holocaust Industry and zionism itself are not the machinations of 'organized American jewry', but of the anglo-european imperialist bourgeoisie, which is much more vast and powerful than the jewish bourgeosie alone. <br /><br />Criticisms aside, the Holocaust Industry is an essential work for anyone interested in the history of memory.</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1177903682" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1177903682" />
    <a title="Mehdi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5165374-mehdi"><img alt="Mehdi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1382037003p2/5165374.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1177903682?book_show_action=true">Jan 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mehdi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mehdi" href="/user/show/5165374-mehdi">Mehdi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1177903682" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10060761739221485845">I picked up Mr. Finkelstein's book because it is deeply divisive, with some admonishing the author as "paranoid", "fanatical" (Omer Bartov, Israeli military historian) and an "obvious crackpot" (Gabriel Schoenfeld), while others lauded it as "the most intelligent political critic in the US". You will likely find that the former have Alan Dershowitz's "Case for Israel" proudly sitting on their bookhself, while the latter likely oppose Zionism in all its forms. Being neither, I approached this boo</span>
  <span id="freeText10060761739221485845" style="display:none">I picked up Mr. Finkelstein's book because it is deeply divisive, with some admonishing the author as "paranoid", "fanatical" (Omer Bartov, Israeli military historian) and an "obvious crackpot" (Gabriel Schoenfeld), while others lauded it as "the most intelligent political critic in the US". You will likely find that the former have Alan Dershowitz's "Case for Israel" proudly sitting on their bookhself, while the latter likely oppose Zionism in all its forms. Being neither, I approached this book with a truly open mind. <br /><br />The outcome? Well, there's a lot of good in "The Holocaust Industry", as well as a lot of bad - thus the three-star rating (2.5 stars may have been more adequate, but goodreads doesn't offer the option). Before I go into a more in-depth discussion, I would like to make three critical points. First, No, Finkelstein is absolutey not an antisemite - or at least, there is nothing in this book that can be construed as antisemitism. Second, Finkelstein is indeed extremely critical of Israel, and there is evidence of an anti-zionist stance throughout the book. Last but not least, the book does not in any way, shape or form attempt to minimize or question the Nazi Holocaust - rather, it is a commentary on the way the event was historicized and, in Finkelstein's view, recuperated by Jews as well and the state of Israel.<br /><br />The book is organized in three main chapters. Each deals with a well-defined topic, and can be read in isolation. As such, each deserves its own analysis and rating. Chapter 1 gets a "1", Chapter 2 gets a "3" and Chapter 3 gets a "4" - averaging to a 2.5 or so<br /><br />In the first chapter ("Capitalizing the Holocaust"), Finkelstein argues that the Holocaust was only construed as a historical reality in the 1960s. He also defends the opinion that Israel only became important to American Jews following the Arab-Israeli war in 1967. This is by far the weakest chapter of the book. While the argument is novel, the evidence presented is rather weak and "negative" (i.e., the absence of visible support for Israel and absence of significant Jewish scholarship on the Holocaust serves as proof). Finkelstein also readily dismisses the view that repressed memory in a trauma may account for the delay. I am sorry Finkelstein, but it is likely that - just as in any trauma - framing the Nazi Holocaust did take time and introspection. This is also the shortest chapter, and very much feels like a botched job.<br /><br />I have mixed feeling about the second chapter ("Hoaxers, Hucksters and History"). Finkelstein makes a potent argument about the framing of the Holocaust as both 1) a unique historical event, like no other and 2) the climax of a historical, millenial-old anti-semitic sentiment in Europe. Finkelstein rightly remarks that the Holocaust is then portrayed as an Absolute Evil, one that bears no comparison, making any historiographic work around it sacrilegious. These claims, Finkelstein then argues, are then used to give the state of Israel an incompromissible authoritarian hold over its morality, thereby making any and all criticism of the Jewish state akin to a reenactement of the Jewish genocide (and thus, becomes antisemitism). There is value in this argument, and Finkelstein brings powerful examples - for instance, on how display of non-Jewish victims of the Holocaust in Holocaust museums around the United States is the result of the deliberate efforts of the like of Elie Wisel (evidence is provided a-plenty). The discussion of two fraudlent survivor accounts also adds fuel to the fire: it is not so much that these books are scandalous frauds that constitutes a problem, but the fact that their content and authors were publicly defended even after the fraud had been exposed. So why 3 stars? Well, for one, the style is unnecessarily polemical and defensive. In a very unscholarly fashion, Finkelstein consistently makes jabs at Israel, which detracts greatly from the argument presented here. Perhaps most importantly, Mr. Finkelstein consistently refers to a Holocaust industry and comes out as a conspiracy theorist. His argument does make sense, but I personnally believe that what happened is the result of an accidental congruence of views, interests and behaviors of individuals rather than the outcome of some politically-planned campaign by the state of Israel.<br /><br />Last but not least, Chapter 3 ("The double shakedown") is the best of the book. Its argument is most novel - Holocaust survivors (including Finkelstein's parents) were robbed of Holocaust reparations as much by Jewish organizations claiming to act on their behalf (and who diverted the funds to various Jewish and pro-Israel causes) as they were by the various states that persecuted them. He also argues that such organizations indulged in unwarranted litigations, leveraging political goodwill to extort funds from various countries and companies. This chapter is extremely well-researched, with an overwhelming - and ultimaetly very difficult to question - set of evidence. Several prominent Holocaust scholars who were otherwise critical of the book applauded Finkelstein's accomplishment here. Raul Hilberg states: "I refer now to the part of the book that deals with the claims against the Swiss banks, and the other claims pertaining to forced labor. I would now say in retrospect that he was actually conservative, moderate and that his conclusions are trustworthy. He is a well-trained political scientist, has the ability to do the research, did it carefully, and has come up with the right results." I give this chapter only four stars for two reasons: first, I feel that at times Finkelstein is overly complacent to countries like Switzerland in their role in the Holocaust. Second, the style feels very dry and the whole thing reads like a law journal. However, I would argue this ultimately supports the argmuent made here.<br /><br />So here you have it. A mixed review of a book that elicits anything but mixed reviews. I suppose I must be a contrarian.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10060761739221485845" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2805497302" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2805497302" />
    <a title="Locky" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/72688797-locky"><img alt="Locky" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559244127p2/72688797.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2805497302?book_show_action=true">Aug 24, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Locky" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Locky" href="/user/show/72688797-locky">Locky</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/72688797-locky?shelf=read-in-2019">read-in-2019</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2805497302" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15934119153209282750">I've got a lot to say about the topic of holocaust reparations as it's something I've studied out of sheer interest, which I'll tie in with this book review. Strap in, this is going to be a long review.<br/><br/>I'll give Finkelstein credit that he's probably the first person (at least that I know of) to blow the whistle on the holocaust reparations racket in a major way (and definitely the first Jew to do so).<br/>Finkelstein does a great job in exposing a few of the many holocaust shucksters such as Elie Wie</span>
  <span id="freeText15934119153209282750" style="display:none">I've got a lot to say about the topic of holocaust reparations as it's something I've studied out of sheer interest, which I'll tie in with this book review. Strap in, this is going to be a long review.<br /><br />I'll give Finkelstein credit that he's probably the first person (at least that I know of) to blow the whistle on the holocaust reparations racket in a major way (and definitely the first Jew to do so).<br />Finkelstein does a great job in exposing a few of the many holocaust shucksters such as Elie Wiesel. Not only does he expose Wiesel as a liar (Wiesel claims to have read Kant's 'The Critique of Pure Reason' in Yiddish as a teenager straight out of Auschwitz, even though it had not been translated into Yiddish at that time), he also reveals Wiesel's greed (he was demanding a $25,000 speaking fee per engagement as well as a chauffered limousine for transport to the venue).<br />Using Wiesel's works as an example, Finkelstein also goes on to show how the holocaust has become a uniquely terrible event in history to Jews which can never be paralleled nor compared to in any way. Forget the Holodomor, the Rwandan genocide, the nukes dropped on Japan... Finkelstein makes the point that many Jews consider it anti-Semitic to even compare these events to the holocaust.<br />In fact, a recent poll questioned Jews on what the most important thing about being Jewish is, and the number one thing, receiving a whole 73% of the vote, was 'The Holocaust'.<br />The book also does a decent job in explaining the Jewish love of victimhood, but not to the degree of which Kevin MacDonald does in 'The Culture of Critique'.<br /><br />Finkelstein also illuminates the discrepancies in the number of Holocaust survivors - at one point, Jewish organisations and historians claimed the number to have walked out from the camps to be at about 20,000 individuals. As this book progresses, Finkelstein notes how that number jumped up to over 900,000 as reparations became a reality.<br />It's important to note here that the definition of holocaust survivor was changed by these Jewish organisations so that even Jews serving in the Red Army were considered holocaust survivors, due to the fact that they might have been put into camps if the Germans ever took them hostage.<br />Since the writing of this book in the early 2000s, the definition of holocaust survivor has once more been modified - I recently discovered that those who were just a fetus in their mother's womb while she was in a concentration camp during WWII are now considered survivors of the holocaust and are eligible for compensation from the German government (and as of last month, so too are the partners of holocaust survivors eligible for nine months of compensation if the survivor is to pass away).<br /><br />Speaking of compensation from the German government, Israel claims to have over 200,000 holocaust survivors still living within her borders and will receive over $560 million dollars in reparations this year (2019) alone. That brings the total amount of restitution paid by Germany to approximately 100 billion dollars. Someone please remind these people that the war ended 74 years ago.<br />More instances of Jewish demands for reparations since publication of this book include the French national railway being collectively sued for compensation, a Dutch railway being sued in the same manner, a current lawsuit against Hungary where claimants want 'tens of billions of dollars' in return for Hungary's cooperation with Nazi Germany (this last case was actually green lit by the judicial system in the US). <br /><br />Back to Finkelstein's book. 'The Holocaust Industry' focusses mostly on Swiss bank reparations, which is alright, but it severely misses out on an opportunity to undermine the holocaust as a whole (which is probably not the intention of the Jewish writer). <br />There's no mention of the ludicrous claims made by Jews of the happenings within the concentration camps - the soap bars made of Jews and lampshades of Jewish skin, the masturbation machines, the stairs of death, the holocoaster, the electric floors, the eagle and the bear ring and so on (google any of these claims if you're unfamiliar with them), nor much emphasis on Hollywood's love of propagandising the holocaust.<br />Finkelstein also claims early in the book that 'after 1967, Israel facilitated assimilation in the United States; Jews now stood on the front lines defending America - indeed 'western civilization' - against the retrograde Arab hordes.' This is blatantly false. Jews are underrepresented in the military, and Israel has never cooperated in defending American interests - just look at the Lavon affair, or the USS Liberty incident, or the claims about Saddam's nuclear stockpile, or today's Jewish warmongering against Iran. America serves Israel's interests, and not the other way around.<br />There's also frequent justifications made for reparations to blacks and Indians in America - if the Jews get their payday, why not the blacks and Indians too, suggests the author.<br />Another gripe I have with the book is its readability. All too often it reads like the terms and conditions of an iTunes account when there's so many opportunities to add context and a bit of flavour to the issues at hand.<br /><br />A more appropriate title of this book would be 'The Swiss bank shakedown', as most of it deals with the pressure placed on Swiss banks to pay large amounts of money for fraudulent claims of persecution.<br />It's a book worth reading as it really does confirm the Jewish stereotype of the love of money and of playing the victim, which some people are yet to accept, but for people who've read a little about the behaviour of these people, it's nothing surprising and not the book it really could be.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15934119153209282750" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/878236" />
    <a title="Abby" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69397-abby"><img alt="Abby" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1179869745p2/69397.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/878236?book_show_action=true">Apr 25, 2007</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Abby" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Abby" href="/user/show/69397-abby">Abby</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">mainly other Jews, but anyone who knows anything about Jews, the Holocaust, or Israel</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69397-abby?shelf=non-fiction">non-fiction</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer878236" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16656506286918810367">Norm Finkelstein thoroughly documented a phenomenon that has been nagging at me for a while now, which is the exploitation of the history of persecution of the Jews. As the oldest grandchild of Holocaust survivors, I have never questioned the horrors that my grandparents experienced. What Professor Finkelstein documents is how this horror has been used as a muzzle and a tool, in ways more extreme than I had even realized. <br/><br/>When I began advocating for human rights in Israel and Palestine, I realiz</span>
  <span id="freeText16656506286918810367" style="display:none">Norm Finkelstein thoroughly documented a phenomenon that has been nagging at me for a while now, which is the exploitation of the history of persecution of the Jews. As the oldest grandchild of Holocaust survivors, I have never questioned the horrors that my grandparents experienced. What Professor Finkelstein documents is how this horror has been used as a muzzle and a tool, in ways more extreme than I had even realized. <br /><br />When I began advocating for human rights in Israel and Palestine, I realized that the Holocaust was one of the sharpest weapons in the "Anti-Semitism" defense that supporters of Israel's current policies throw at anyone who dares suggest that maybe, just maybe, Israel should: obey the laws of war or indeed any international law,and question whether the whole "Jewish state" concept might be a bit discriminatory on its face and in its enforcement. We say, "The IDF shouldn't have shot that 12 year old Palestinian in the head," and we hear, "The Israeli state must be strong, 'they' want to exterminate the Jews." A terrifying thought, if true, but even the most horrid Palestinian terror acts bear no semblence to the system of European pograms, discriminatory laws, and mass murder. (As my grandmother, a survivor of the Lodz ghetto, observed, it is the Occupied Palestinian territories that look a bit like the ghetto. . . And it was an IDF commander who admitted to taking tactics from the Nazis, not a Palestinian militant.)<br /> <br />What made me feel a little more ill is Professor Finkelstein's detailed accounts of how Holocaust litigation has been focused against Swiss banks (even though American and even Israeli banks took Jewish assets during WWII and haven't returned them), how this litigation is framed (as restitution and remedy for needy Holocaust survivors), and where the money goes (not to my grandma, or Norm's parents, but to the Holocaust industry museums and of course Zionist institutions.)<br /><br />He is a stellar historian; I am not. So read the book.<br /> </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_2153709734" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2153709734" />
    <a title="Supriyo Chaudhuri" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/58305-supriyo-chaudhuri"><img alt="Supriyo Chaudhuri" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1176474937p2/58305.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2153709734?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Supriyo Chaudhuri" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Supriyo Chaudhuri" href="/user/show/58305-supriyo-chaudhuri">Supriyo Chaudhuri</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781781685617" href="/book/show/21972002-the-holocaust-industry">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2153709734" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17871657979455492767">If Holocaust is depressing, the exposition of the Holocaust Industry is even more so. I have been told to read 'sensibly' about Holocaust, as there is a lot of trash out there, and I guess this book may be considered beyond the pale by many interested in Holocaust. But, I found this book reasoned and very well argued; polemical perhaps, but the author set out to debunk and polemics was inevitable. A lot of this book is about money, the expropriation of reparation by American Jewish organisations</span>
  <span id="freeText17871657979455492767" style="display:none">If Holocaust is depressing, the exposition of the Holocaust Industry is even more so. I have been told to read 'sensibly' about Holocaust, as there is a lot of trash out there, and I guess this book may be considered beyond the pale by many interested in Holocaust. But, I found this book reasoned and very well argued; polemical perhaps, but the author set out to debunk and polemics was inevitable. A lot of this book is about money, the expropriation of reparation by American Jewish organisations, which keeps most of the money to itself and fund the ongoing Holocaust spectacle, with support from American political elite. My interests were, however, different, in the history of Holocaust, and yet I found enough here to justify the labour of reading. In my mind now, there are two Holocausts: One of history, the murder of millions of non-combatants in Europe between 1941 and 1945; and the other one, as a cultural artefact, an elaborate but purposeful recalibration of History to serve the cause of Israel and American interests in the Middle East. The main difference, from my vantage point, was that, in the Holocaust as history, there were particular perpetrators, the Nazis and their collaborators, and universal suffering, of Jews, Refugees, the Disabled, of Russians and other Slavic peoples, and of political dissidents. In Holocaust as an artefact, this is reversed: There is particular suffering, of the Jews, and universal guilt, of everyone else. In the latter incarnation, Holocaust is an unique event no parallels in history, and yet this must be universally remembered and atoned. For me, this is the paradox of Holocaust: Looking at it from the perspective of an Asian, Holocaust was very much a vast colonial atrocity, unique in its horror, but not so in its imagination or design; one that has lessons for all of us, because it touches lives everywhere. This book allowed me to understand the motives behind the particularisation of the Holocaust.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17871657979455492767" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5640968602981362144">Great book, though I didn't feel the desire to read the post-script before accepting Finkelstein's point about the black-mailing of Swiss banks by Jewish organisations. <br/><br/>Anyhow, I hope more people read this book and appreciate that the Holocaust should be studied rationally and objectively, and that we shouldn't let people's sensibilities and emotions around it hijack its discussion.   <span id="freeText5640968602981362144" style="display:none">Great book, though I didn't feel the desire to read the post-script before accepting Finkelstein's point about the black-mailing of Swiss banks by Jewish organisations. <br /><br />Anyhow, I hope more people read this book and appreciate that the Holocaust should be studied rationally and objectively, and that we shouldn't let people's sensibilities and emotions around it hijack its discussion. Among many things, this means acknowledging and giving due attention to other genocides that have occurred in history, and it also means that people should stop levelling accusations of anti-semitism to critics of Israeli government policy or use the Holocaust as an excuse or justification for anything Jew-related. Criticising the building of Israeli settlements in the West Bank does not make you a racist.<br /></span>

<div id="review_2987830496" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Shivangi Jain" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/71925067-shivangi-jain"><img alt="Shivangi Jain" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540791787p2/71925067.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2987830496?book_show_action=true">May 31, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shivangi Jain" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shivangi Jain" href="/user/show/71925067-shivangi-jain">Shivangi Jain</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer2987830496&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2987830496" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10975667297774966053">Never have I ever read a book before that I have been so conflicted about.<br/><br/>The book addresses 3 main things-<br/>1.Post-WW2, a lot of Jewish organizations "unjustly" shook down and thug Switzerland and other bordering nations for monetary compensation for way more than that was taken away from them. These organizations were assisted by the US in exchange for a military and political alliance with Israel , even though the US itself has engaged and profited from horrific human rights violations (slavery</span>
  <span id="freeText10975667297774966053" style="display:none">Never have I ever read a book before that I have been so conflicted about.<br /><br />The book addresses 3 main things-<br />1.Post-WW2, a lot of Jewish organizations "unjustly" shook down and thug Switzerland and other bordering nations for monetary compensation for way more than that was taken away from them. These organizations were assisted by the US in exchange for a military and political alliance with Israel , even though the US itself has engaged and profited from horrific human rights violations (slavery) and never paid any sort of reparations.<br />2. The shake down money was used unjustly by certain individuals and organizations for their own profit rather than be distributed amongst Holocaust survivors, as was promised<br />3. The Holocaust is potrayed as being the ultimate genocide because of which any mention of the atrocities of the crimes committed by Jews is linked to anti-semitism. One is not allowed to speak ill of the happenings in Palestine for the fear of being called anti-semitic. <br /><br />In totality, the book talks about the Holocaust being used as an industry for undue enrichment of some.<br /><br />While I see where the author is coming from in regards to the crimes committed by Israelis in Palestine, I do not see eye to eye with him about anywhere else. I do not think that any amount of money can compensate for the suffering and loss of life that took place. I especially abhorred the hinting towards how one specific genocide could take all the money while there are so many others that have not been paid reparations at all.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10975667297774966053" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('VyVVpjjANUScExZq+OV022sJsWo6bu8fshgIzp12f1vwIqm1grN870YuWHBqqkg5rXaoKNpLa6xUQluTfLAspQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

Originally published in the London Review of<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText10497315986197969279\" style=\"display:none\">\n  The Israel Lobby,&quot; by John J. Mearsheimer of the University of Chicago and Stephen M. Walt of Harvard\'s John F. Kennedy School of Government, was one of the most controversial articles in recent memory. Originally published in the London Review of Books in March 2006, it provoked both howls of outrage and cheers of gratitude for challenging what had been a taboo issue in America: the impact of the Israel lobby on U.S. foreign policy. \n   \n  Now in a work of major importance, Mearsheimer and Walt deepen and expand their argument and confront recent developments in Lebanon and Iran. They describe the remarkable level of material and diplomatic support that the United States provides to Israel and argues that this support cannot be fully explained on either strategic or moral grounds. This exceptional relationship is due largely to the political influence of a loose coalition of individuals and organizations that actively work to shape U.S. foreign policy in a pro-Israel direction. Mearsheimer and Walt provocatively contend that the lobby has a far-reaching impact on America\'s posture throughout the Middle East--in Iraq, Iran, Lebanon, and toward the Israeli-Palestinian conflict--and the policies it has encouraged are in neither America\'s national interest nor Israel\'s long-term interest. The lobby\'s influence also affects America\'s relationship with important allies and increases dangers that all states face from global jihadist terror. \n   \n  Writing in The New York Review of Books, Michael Massing declared, &quot;Not since Foreign Affairs magazine published Samuel Huntington\'s \'The Clash of Civilizations?\' in 1993 has an academic essay detonated with such force.&quot; But when utopian programs clash with dissenters—and with reality itself—the result is chaos, which revolutionaries seek to quash with repression and terror. In Sexual Utopia in Power, F. Roger Devlin explores today’s sexual dystopia, with its loose morals and confused sexual roles; its soaring rates of divorce, celibacy, and childlessness; and the increasingly arbitrary and punitive attempts to regulate and police it. Devlin shows that the breakdown of monogamy results in promiscuity for the few, loneliness for the majority, and unhappiness for all.  Every revolution gives rise to a reaction. Devlin, however, is very critical of mainstream conservative responses to the sexual revolution, which often eerily echo feminist complaints about innocent women being preyed upon by wicked men who must be scolded and punished. The most controversial aspect of Devlin’s work is his argument that today’s sexual dystopia is rooted just as much in women’s nature as men’s, exploring such taboo topics as female hypergamy (mating up), narcissism, infidelity, deceptiveness, and masochism. By showing their biological basis, F. Roger Devlin offers a non-traditional defense of traditional sexual morals and institutions and shows us the way out of today’s sexual dystopia. During both wars, fantastic atrocity stories were invented by Allied propaganda to create hatred of the German people for the purpose of bringing public opinion around to support the wars. The &quot;Holocaust&quot; propaganda which emerged after World War II further solidified this image of Germany as history\'s ultimate villain. But how true is this &quot;official&quot; story? Was Germany really history\'s ultimate villain? In this book, the author paints a different picture. He explains that Germany was not the perpetrator of World War I nor World War II, but instead, was the victim of Allied aggression in both wars. The instability wrought by World War I made the 1917 Bolshevik Revolution in Russia possible, which brought world Communism into existence. Hitler and Germany recognized world Communism, with its base in the Soviet Union, as an existential threat to Western, Christian Civilization, and he dedicated himself and Germany to a death struggle against it. Far from being the disturber of European peace, Germany served as a bulwark which prevented Communist revolution from sweeping over Europe. The pity was that the United States and Britain did not see Communist Russia in the same light, ultimately with disastrous consequences for Western Civilization. He also maps out the external and internal forces that destroyed communism, and the disastrous impact of the “free-market” victory on eastern Europe and the former Soviet Union. He affirms the relevance of taboo ideologies like Marxism, demonstrating the importance of class analysis in understanding political realities and dealing with the ongoing collision between ecology and global corporatism.\n\nWritten with lucid and compelling style, this book goes beyond truncated modes of thought, inviting us to entertain iconoclastic views, and to ask why things are as they are. It is a bold and entertaining exploration of the epic struggles of yesterday and today.\n\n&quot;A penetrating and persuasive writer with an astonishing array of documentation to implement his attacks.&quot;—The Catholic Journalist\n\n&quot;Blackshirts &amp; Reds discusses the great combat between fascism and socialism that is the defining feature of the Twentieth Century, and takes every official version to task for its substitution of moral analysis for critical analysis, for its selectivity, and for its errata. By portraying the struggle between fascism and Communism in this century as a single conflict, and not a series of discrete encounters, between the insatiable need for new capital on the one hand and the survival of a system under siege on the other, Parenti defines fascism as the weapon of capitalism, not simply an extreme form of it. In this, his adaptation and interpretation of it, Yukio Mishima deals with its teachings on action, subjectivity, strength of character, passion and love, and delights in giving prolific examples of Jōchō’s practical advice from proper behavior at a drinking party to child rearing. In the Hagakure, the most important influence on his life – and his death – Mishima saw striking similarities between his criticisms of materialistic post-war Japan and Jōchō’s criticisms of the A Nobel laureate deeply beloved by his countrymen, Hamsun was now<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText16310181573260814192\" style=\"display:none\">On Overgrown Paths was written after World War II, at a time when Hamsun was in police custody for his openly expressed Nazi sympathies during the German occupation of Norway, 1940-45. A Nobel laureate deeply beloved by his countrymen, Hamsun was now reviled as a traitor—as long as his sanity was not called into question. On Overgrown Paths is Hamsun\'s apologia.However, the psychiatric report declared him to be sane, but concluded that his mental faculties were &quot;permanently impaired.&quot; This conclusion was emphatically refuted by the publication, in 1949, of On Overgrown Paths, Hamsun\'s apologia. In its creative élan, this book, filled with the proud sorrow of an old man, miraculously recalls the spirit of Hamsun\'s early novels, with their reverence for nature, absurdist humor, and quirky flights of fancy.This edition is the first authoritative English translation of Hamsun\'s last work, a work which stood at the center of the recent film Hamsun.Knut Hamsun was the greatest 20th century Norwegian novelist, winner of the Nobel Prize, and enormously beloved when the country was occupied in World War II. During the war, however, his wife, a supporter of Quisling and the Nazis, traveled across the country reading from his work, particularly Growth of the Soil, which seemed to support notions of agrarian return by a superior Aryan peasant class. Old and confused, Hamsun traveled to Germany to meet with Hitler, hoping, he claimed, to change the conditions of occupation in Norway. The meeting ended disastrously, and after the war, Hamsun was arrested for his Nazi sympathy. As this book reveals, however, Hamsun was anything by mentally disturbed. It is a sad and tragic book filled with pained sorrow of an old man, great in stature and contribution, but completely out of touch with his own time.<\/span>\n  <a <span id="freeTextContainer11795956374094649049">Norman Finkelstein, son of a holocaust survivor, is a fierce and controversial critic of Israeli policy, especially toward Palestinians. He has had a tense rivalry with his pro-Israel counterpart, Alan Dershowitz. In 2007 DePaul University denied his tenure, a decision for which Dershowitz lobbied. For his views and suspected connections to anti-Zionist groups, Israel has denied Finkelstein entry </span>
  <span id="freeText11795956374094649049" style="display:none">Norman Finkelstein, son of a holocaust survivor, is a fierce and controversial critic of Israeli policy, especially toward Palestinians. He has had a tense rivalry with his pro-Israel counterpart, Alan Dershowitz. In 2007 DePaul University denied his tenure, a decision for which Dershowitz lobbied. For his views and suspected connections to anti-Zionist groups, Israel has denied Finkelstein entry and banned him from the country for a decade.</span>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/1611039-the-holocaust-industry-reflections-on-the-exploitation-of-jewish-suffer">Quotes from The Holocaust Ind...</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Manifest Destiny anticipated nearly all the ideological and programmatic elements of Hitler's Lebensraum policy. In fact, Hitler modeled his conquest of the East on the American conquest of the West.* During the first half of this century, a majority of American states enacted sterilization laws and tens of thousands of Americans were involuntarily sterilized. The Nazis explicitly invoked this US precedent when they enacted their own sterilization laws.'' The notorious 1935 Nuremberg Laws stripped Jews of the franchise and forbade miscegenation between Jews and non-Jews. Blacks in the American South suffered the same legal disabilities and were the object of much greater spontaneous and sanctioned popular violence than the Jews in prewar Germany.<br /> To highlight unfolding crimes abroad, the US often summons memories of The Holocaust. The more revealing point, however, is when the US invokes The Holocaust. Crimes of official enemies such as the Khmer Rouge bloodbath in Cambodia, the Soviet invasion of Afghanistan, the Iraqi invasion of Kuwait, and Serbian ethnic cleansing in Kosovo recall The Holocaust; crimes in which the US is complicit do not.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/1140317-manifest-destiny-anticipated-nearly-all-the-ideological-and-programmatic-elements">5 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;It is important to recognize that our efforts at communal property restitution,” Stuart Eizenstat told a House committee, “are integral to the rebirth and renewal of Jewish life” in Eastern Europe. Allegedly to “promote the revival” of Jewish life in Poland, the World Jewish Restitution Organization is demanding title over the 6,000 prewar communal Jewish properties, including those currently being used as hospitals and schools. The prewar Jewish population of Poland stood at 3.5 million; the current population is several thousand. Does reviving Jewish life really require one synagogue or school building per Polish Jew? The organization is also laying claim to hundreds of thousands of parcels of Polish land valued in the many tens of billions of dollars. “Polish officials fear,” Jewish Week reports, that the demand “could bankrupt the nation.” When Poland’s Parliament proposed limits on compensation to avert insolvency, Elan Steinberg of the WJC denounced the legislation as “fundamentally an anti-American act.”80&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/9252617-it-is-important-to-recognize-that-our-efforts-at-communal">1 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
        <a class="actionLink" style="float: right" href="/work/quotes/1611039-the-holocaust-industry-reflections-on-the-exploitation-of-jewish-suffer">More quotes&hellip;</a>
